<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Dansk National Sang af Juliane Marie Jessen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>

<th>Composer

<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voice, piano - arranged for male chorus or wind band or orchestra
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Jessen's text was the winner of a competition on a new Danish national anthem held in 1818 by the society, 'Selskabet til de skiønne og nyttige Videnskabers Forfremmelse' (The Society for the promotion of the fine and useful arts).
<p>The winner of the subsequent competition for the best tune was <i><a href="/wiki/Nationalsang_(Weyse,_Christoph_Ernst_Friedrich)" title="Nationalsang (Weyse, Christoph Ernst Friedrich)">Nationalsang</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Category:Weyse,_Christoph_Ernst_Friedrich" title="Category:Weyse, Christoph Ernst Friedrich">Christoph Ernst Friedrich Weyse</a> (1774-1842). Gerson's tune may have been among the 24 submitted compositions. At least its settings adhere more or less to the competition conditions: a score for grand orchestra, a score for a military wind orchestra, and a score for 3-4 singers with piano accompaniment. Further studies in the archive of the society are required. See Jørgen Poul Erichsen, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://tidsskrift.dk/index.php/fundogforskning/article/viewFile/1719/2882">Den kronede danske nationalsang fra 1819 og hvad deraf fulgte, en litterær pennefejde med et musikalsk efterspil</a> in'Fund og Forskning', vol. 22, 1976.
<br />The instrument <i>corno basso</i> was developed from the serpent around 1800. See Curt Sachs, Handbuch der Musikinstrumentenkunde, Leipzig 1930, p. 264f and the German Wikipedia article on <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/de:Basshorn" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:de:Basshorn">Basshorn</a>
</p>
</td></tr></table>
</div>
<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Tagged as a song, not a national anthem, because the official national anthems of Denmark (there are 2) both seem to have different words, so it does not seem that the winning anthem was ever used as an official anthem.
</p>
